<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">ITEM
2.02.&#160; <i><font style="font-style:italic;">RESULTS
OF OPERATIONS AND FINANCIAL CONDITION</font></i></font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">On September&nbsp;9,
2004, Cutter &amp; Buck Inc. issued a press release announcing its financial
results for the first quarter of fiscal 2005 and an increase in its quarterly
dividend.&#160; A copy of the press release is
furnished as Exhibit 99.1 and shall not be deemed &quot;filed&quot; for the
purposes of Section 18 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended, or
otherwise subject to the liabilities of that Section.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">ITEM
7.01. <i><font style="font-style:italic;">REGULATION FD DISCLOSURE</font></i></font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">On September 9, 2004,
Cutter &amp; Buck Inc. issued a press release announcing its financial results
for the first quarter of fiscal 2005 and an increase in its quarterly
dividend.&#160; The information in this
Current Report is being furnished and shall not be deemed &#147;filed&#148; for the
purposes of Section&nbsp;18 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended,
or otherwise subject to the liabilities of that Section.&#160; The information in this Current Report shall
not be incorporated by reference into any registration statement or other
document pursuant to the Securities Act of 1933, as amended, except as shall be
expressly set forth by specific reference in such filing.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">ITEM 9.01.&#160; <i><font style="font-style:italic;">FINANCIAL
STATEMENTS AND EXHIBITS</font></i></font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(c)&#160; EXHIBITS</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-family:Times New Roman;font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">99.1</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Press
Release dated September&nbsp;9, 2004, furnished pursuant to Items 2.02 and 7.01
of this Form 8-K announcing financial results for the first quarter of fiscal
2005 and an increase in the company&#146;s quarterly dividend.</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">MANAGEMENT
VIEWPOINT:</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The first quarter of the fiscal year shows a continuation of recent
quarters&#146; results, as we benefit from our ongoing efforts to upgrade business
processes.&#160; We produced pre-tax income
in our ongoing wholesale business of $5.1 million, up from $3.2 million in the
first quarter of the prior year (Table B).&#160;&#160;
Our gross margins are up, and our operating expenses are down. Our
balance sheet is strong, with inventory levels down $5.2 million and free cash
flow up $2.6 million compared to the first quarter of last year. This quarter
marks our sixth consecutive quarter of profitability.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We are generally pleased with our financial results for the first
quarter of fiscal 2005. Net sales grew in most of our target markets.&#160; The exception is our golf market, where we
are disappointed</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>


<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">

<hr size="2" width="100%" noshade color="gray" align="left">

</font></div>

<p align="center" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">with results.&#160; To turn this
around, we are bringing in a new manager for the golf unit, adding a senior
golf merchandiser, reviewing our sales operations and programs, examining our
product offerings, increasing our marketing activities, and enhancing our
customer service.&#160; These initiatives
have long lead times, and we expect that it will take time for our efforts to
produce favorable results.&#160; We continue
to see that many upscale golf customers and consumers have strong loyalty to
our brand.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">During the quarter, the new &#147;Annika by Cutter &amp; Buck&#148; line came to
golf shops, and both customers and consumers appear to be receiving it
enthusiastically.&#160; The new &#147;Integrity
Pique&#148; shirt, made with 100% organic cotton, was available toward the end of
the quarter, and early indications are that there is a good and growing market for
this innovative product, which combines Cutter &amp; Buck&#146;s trademark style and
comfort with our commitment to social responsibility.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">CEO TRANSITION AND SEARCH FOR A
NEW CEO</font></u></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">As previously announced, on September&nbsp;16<sup>th</sup> Fran Conley
will be leaving as Chairman and Chief Executive Officer.&#160; Doug Southern will become Chairman of the
Board, and Bill Swint will become interim Chief Executive Officer.&#160; The transitions are proceeding smoothly and
we are pleased that the company has such skilled managers available to keep its
momentum going while we search for a permanent CEO.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Doug Southern commented, &#147;The board and employees of Cutter &amp; Buck
wish to thank Fran for her years of service on the board of directors, and in
particular for her recent role as CEO.&#160;
She took over during a time of crisis and successfully navigated the
company to its current position of strength and profitability.&#148;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&#147;Cutter &amp; Buck&#146;s most important current priority,&#148; Southern
continued, &#147;is to hire a permanent Chief Executive Officer who is an extraordinary
person who can lead and build the company in the future.&#160; As previously announced, the company has
hired the Russell Reynolds search firm to assist it in this endeavor and we are
already reviewing candidates.&#148;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">FISCAL
YEAR 2005</font></u></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">During this transition
period, we intend to move forward firmly on the strategy now in place:&#160; to maintain the integrity and upscale
positioning of the Cutter &amp; Buck brand while we continue to strengthen the
company&#146;s foundations.&#160; This year&#146;s
projects are planned to include the installation of new major computer systems
and documentation of internal controls to comply with the Sarbanes-Oxley Act of
2002, particularly Section&nbsp;404.&#160;&#160;
Both of these projects will add operating expenses above those of last
year.&#160; In addition, we plan to increase
our spending on marketing to bring our great brand more effectively to the
attention of our customers and consumers.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">We continue to be cautious about
sales levels. Our markets seem more robust and our brand is strong, but we are
not currently anticipating significant growth this year, particularly in light
of</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>


<div><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">

<hr size="2" width="100%" noshade color="gray" align="left">

</font></div>

<font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">
<!-- SEQ.=1,FOLIO='',FILE='C:\jms\mramana\04-10387-1\task182657\10387-1-mm.htm',USER='mrnathan',CD='Sep  9 14:49 2004' -->
<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">
</font>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">our recent golf results.&#160; We do believe, however, that we are laying a
strong foundation for future sales growth.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The levels of sales and gross
margins in first quarter should not be taken as predictive of future
results.&#160;&#160;&#160; Each of our markets has its
own seasonality, and as the mix of sales changes, our seasonality may change.
In addition, we are managing the schedule&nbsp;for liquidation of products
differently to realize maximum value, which may impact the seasonality of gross
margins.&#160;&#160; For the balance of the year,
we currently anticipate that our margins will range between 45% and 48%.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Until the
permanent CEO is in place and has had the opportunity to work with the board on
charting the company&#146;s strategic direction, we plan to maintain our strategic
flexibility, and generally to maintain our current direction, cash balances,
and capital structure.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">DIVIDEND AND STOCK REPURCHASE
PROGRAM</font></u></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Two quarters ago, the board of
directors initiated both a quarterly dividend and a stock repurchase
program.&#160; Today we announce an increase
in the dividend, from $.05 to $.07 a share. The board of directors has approved
a dividend of $0.07 a share, payable on October&nbsp;8, 2004 to shareholders of
record on September&nbsp;24, 2004.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">During the first quarter, we
purchased 16,800 shares of our common stock at an average price of $10.48.&#160; Since the inception of our stock repurchase
program, we repurchased a total of 73,626 shares of our common stock at an
average price of $10.27.&#160; We still have
$5.2 million available in the program for share repurchases, and we remain
committed to purchasing shares at times and prices that are advantageous for
our shareholders.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">ANNUAL MEETING</font></u></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The annual meeting of shareholders will be
held at 9 AM on October&nbsp;21, at the company&#146;s corporate office in Seattle.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Cutter &amp; Buck invites investors to listen to a broadcast of the
company&#146;s conference call to discuss these matters.&#160; The conference call will be broadcast live over the Internet at
11:00 AM Eastern Time, 8:00 AM Pacific Time, September&nbsp;9, 2004.&#160; To listen to the conference call, go to

<p style="font-style:italic;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:normal;">&nbsp;</font></i></p>

<h1 align="left" style="font-weight:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-decoration:underline;"><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">About Cutter &amp; Buck</font></u></h1>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Cutter &amp; Buck designs and markets upscale sportswear under the
Cutter &amp; Buck brand.&#160; The Company
sells its products primarily to golf and specialty retailers, corporations and
international distributors and licensees.&#160;
Cutter &amp; Buck products feature distinctive, comfortable designs,
high quality materials and manufacturing, and rich detailing.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>


<div style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">

</font></div>

<p align="center" style="font-size:10.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Table B:&#160;
Management Viewpoint of Operations and Reconciliation to GAAP Numbers
Above</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.1in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">To understand the performance of our wholesale business, management
considers it useful to review our operating results excluding costs that are
not elements of running our wholesale business on an ongoing basis, such as
restatement expenses.&#160; We adjust our net
income calculated in accordance with generally accepted accounting principles
to exclude income and expense items that are not directly related to our
wholesale business, in order to give us better information regarding the
profitability of our wholesale business. We use this analysis to compare pretax
wholesale business income on a quarterly and year-to-date basis</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Quarter Ended
July&nbsp;31,</font></b></p>
